 is maamle main court se FIR darj karne or court kii nigaraanee main SIT se jaanch kii maang ko khaarij kar diya gaya
 In this petition, while being the Chief Minister of Gujarat, several politicians, including Narendra Modi, were accused of taking bribes citing this diary and urging the court to order an inquiry into it
 apane faisle main supreme court ne kaha ki mahaj diary or kagajaton main naam likhe hone ke aadhaar par jaanch ke aadesh nahin die ja sakate
 According to the court, the facts given in the petition are not admissible
 inako pukhta subut ke taur par nahin gina ja saktaa
 On the basis of such submitted documents and material, there cannot be an inquiry against those sitting in constitutional positions
 is par justise arun mishra ne kaha ki tab to aapako pataa hoga ki jaanch ke aadesh dene ke baad kya hua
 Here the Supreme Court ordered an inquiry, on the other hand, the accused were discharged from the lower court
 jaahir he ki ham nyaaypalika ko virodhabhasi halaat main nahin dekhnaa chaahate
 On the other hand, opposing the petition, Attorney General Mukul Rohatgi opined that the thing written in the diary is no evidence and is not a cognizable offense and thus there should be evidence to prove what is written in the diary
 agar is yachika par jaanch ke aadesh die gaye to desh bhar main aise keson kii bharmaar ho jaaegi
 It is worth mentioning that earlier on the basis of the documents related to the raids of the Income Tax Department, the NGO, which accused Aditya Birla and Sahara group companies of bribing Narendra Modi and other politicians, had told the Supreme Court last Thursday that if the Supreme If the court does not order an inquiry into the matter, no other inquiry will be justified
 vahiin justise jees khehar ne khud ko alag kar liya tha jisase justise arun mishra or justise amitaav raay kii bench main sunwaayee hui
 In fact, during that time, the Supreme Court had asked these documents to present strong evidence to the petitioner organization, declaring them void
 yachikakarta sanghathan sipiiel ne supreme court main halafanama daakhil kar kaha tha ki iskar vibhaag kii aprijal report, diary or i-mail saaf-saaf ishaare karti he ki rajanetaaon ko rishwat di gai thi, lihaaja supreme court ko jaanch kaa aadesh dena chahie
 It is also stated in the affidavit that it rarely happens when such strong documents have been presented to the court or investigating agency
 aise main agar is maamle main jaanch kaa aadesh nahin diya jaataa to supreme court dwaara kisi bhi maamle main jaanch kaa aadesh dena nyaaysangat nahin hoga
 The affidavit states that several other documents, including undisclosed amounts, diaries, notebooks, e-mails were found in the CBI raids on the Birla Group and the Income Tax Department raids on Sahara Group companies

 trai's recent investigation on the services of mobile service providers, as of the end of the quarter of December 2014, shows that only 25 out of 183 networks in the 2G network in the country, ie one in every seven, test the triad of three per cent call drop

 jaankaron kaa kahana he ki samasya kii jad aankadon ke jaal or jatil sarkari nitiyon ke bich kahin fansi padi he

 inamen bhautik infrastracchar ke samaksh khadi chunautiyaan, spectrum kaa abhaav tathaa telecom toweron se vidyut-chumbakeey vikiran se jude masale shaamil hai, jiske chalate logon main yah dharna bani he ki apane gharon ke aasapaas tower nahin lagane dene hai
 There are 4,25,000 Base Transmitting Stations (BTS) in India popularly called mobile phone towers
 mana jaataa he ki mobile phone dharakon kii badhati sankhya ke liye inaki sankhya aparyaapt he
 Hemant Joshi, partner at consulting firm Deloitte, believes that if the quality of transmission of sound and data in India is to improve, then an additional two lakh towers would be needed
 iske liye baari nivesh kii darkaar he kyonki ek tower lagane main 15 se 20 lakh ru
 Costs joshi kehete hai, “telecom companiyon ke munaafe par vaise hi baari chunauti saamne khadi he
 “the telecom industry is currently in debt of two lakh crores, as telecom companies have taken a lot of loans from banks for their expansion
 spectrum main inkaa nivesh to itnaa zyada he ki dimag ko jhakzor degaa
 The telecom companies paid Rs 1 lakh crore to the government for the allocation of spectrum ended in March
 kaa bhugtan kiya he
 Says Joshi, “companies have invested a lot to provide 3G services but they are yet to invest more in towers
 ” teesri peedi kii sevaayen yani 3ji, duusari peedi yani 2ji ke mukaable data hastantaran kii ucch dar muhaiyaa karaati hai lekin bharat ke kul mobile upabhoktaaon main sirf 9 fisadi inke daayre main aate hai
 This number is also not modest
 bharat main mobile par internet kaa prayog karne waalon kii sankhya 25 karod he jo america ke baad duusare sthaan par ise rakhata he or aaj zyada se zyada log duniya se jude rahane ke liye smartphone ke bazaar kaa hissaa ban rahe hai
 With this, the number of people using mobile services in India is increasing rapidly
 bijness or finance paramarshdaata form grant thornton main partner raja lahidi kehete hai, “wais kii lagaataar badhati maang or ab i-commers, sangeet va movie downlod ke tamaam aplicationon ke kaaran badhati data kii maang ke chalate spectrum par dabaav badhata hi ja rahaa he
 While the number of mobile users has grown at a rapid pace, the average charge per consumer needs to be increased
 haalanki yah moolyavardhit sevaaon or data ke kaaran bad hi rahaa he jisase companiyon kii kamai badaae kii sambhaavnaaen paidaa hui hai
 "does radiation cause radiation from mobile phone towers to humans?" Experts around the world believe that there is no evidence of this, so these towers should be considered safe
 bhay ke is maahaul ke aage ghutane tekte hue bharat ke mobile phone seva pradaataaon ne toweron se hone vaale vikiran kii dar ko vaishvik paimaane ke dasven hisse tak gira diya he
 Despite this, there is a fear among the people, due to which many housing societies do not allow these towers to be installed here
 munikh sthit ek sanghathan international kamishan for non yniging radiation (isieniarapy) kaa kaam vikiran ke dushprabhavon par vaigyanik paraamarsh pradaan karnaa he
 Accordingly, the density of energy in a confined space from a telecom tower should be 4,500 milliwatts per square meter
 bharat main iske dasven hisse yani jiesem ke liye 450 millivot prati varg meter ko anumati di gai he jabaki 3ji or 4ji ke liye 1,000 millivot kii anumati he
 Joshi believes that due to such stringent regulation, telecom service providers place fewer towers, due to which their capacity is insufficient and the problem of call drop is created
 graahakon ke maamle main bharat ke duusare sabase bade doorsanchaar seva pradaata vodaphone ke ek pravaktaa kaa kahana he, “vidyut chumbakeey vikiran ke bhay ke kaaran hamen shahari ilaakon main tower lagane ke liye jagahen praapt karne main dikkat aa rahi he
 "he says that to solve this problem, government institutions will have to reach out to the public and spread awareness among them on issues like protection from radiation
 bharat kii sabase badi doorsanchaar seva pradaata company airtel ne is masale par tippanee karne se inkaar kar diya, haalanki company ke chairman sunil mittal ne ek akhabaari saakshaatkaar main june main kaha tha ki kol drop kii samasya se nibatane ke liye unki company vanaweb naam ke ek vaishvik consorcium main alp hissedari kharidne vaali he jo 648 upgrahon ke madhyam se broadband muhaiyaa karaata he
 Under this, a small antenna will be installed on the roofs which will be connected to satellites and will create an automatic base station in the range of 300-400 meters so that connectivity will be maintained on 3G and 4G mobile phones
 bharti interprijej ke vaais chairman or bharti infratel ke kaaryakari adhyaksh akhil gupta ne 3 july ko dilli main yojit digital india kaarykram main siio kii golmes baithak main kaha tha, “main aashwast hum ki kol drop kii samasya kaa samaadhaan nikaala ja sakegaa
 Actually, it troubles us more than people
 ” unhone yah bhi kaha tha ki udyog ko in dushpracharon kaa bhi saamana karnaa pad rahaa he ki tower se “vikiran hota he yaa tower lagane ke liye ham sarkari parisampattiyon” kaa istemaal karnaa chaahate hai
 If the base transmitting station is the direct evidence of the call drop problem, then the invisible evidence is something called spectrum
 spectrum vah vidyut chumbakeey bandwyeth yaa radio tarangen hai jisase mobile phone kii tarangon kaa pareshan hota he
 The government has control over its allocation and the 2G scam and the auction conducted by the NDA government are an indication of how expensive natural resources are
 doorsanchaar sanghathan jieseme ke nideshak sandip karanvaal kehete hai ki dakshin africa, australia yaa malaysia jaise duusare deshon ke mukaable dekhen to bhartiya operataron ke paas uplabdh spectrum kii maatra behad kam he
 In some areas in cities like Mumbai and Delhi, towers are very close to each other, so it becomes impossible to install more towers
 isiilie iklauta vikalp yah he ki operataron ko di gai spectrum kii maatra ko or badha diya jaae
 Says Joshi, "at a time when the world is turning to new technology like 5G, the Indian telecom industry is still struggling to make the necessary investments
 ” ve bataate hai ki duniya kii gati kii barabari karne ke liye bhartiya doorsanchaar udyog ko 6 lakh karod ru
 Requires investment of more than
 bhari tijori, sankara bandspectrum ke maamle main doorsanchaar operataron ke daawey ko chunauti dete hue sarkaar ne unhen peeche dhakelne kaa kaam kiya he
 At the ceo's round table meeting, Telecom Minister Ravi Shankar Prasad stated in stern words that companies have enough spectrum to provide phone services without interruption so they need to fix their systems
 soochna-praudyogiki par sansadeey samiti kii baithak ke das din baad ai is chetavanee ko companiyon ne sahajata se nahin liya he
 The operators, who spoke to India Today, challenged the minister's statement and compared it to international standards here
 unka daawa he ki vaishvik ausat 50 megahertz kaa he jabaki bharat ke oparator 10
 Runs through the spectrum of 5 mhz
 europe main yah 65 megahertz, asia main 45 megahertz or africa main 28 megahertz he
 For example, the available spectrum in Shanghai is two-and-a-half times that of Delhi, although both cities are nearly identical in terms of their size and population density
 bharti airtel ke ek adhyayan ke mutabik, dilli ke network par shanghai ke mukaable 23 guna zyada bhaar he
 Bharti Airtel's network receives one and a half million calls in an hour during peak hours & according to the companies, the busiest hours are between eight to ten in the morning
 companiyon kii shikaayat he ki 2015 kii nilaamee main 3ji operataron ke liye sirf 5 megahertz kii nilaamee kii gai thi
 The thinking within the government is that since spectrum has many uses, telecom companies alone cannot be its consumers and that is why it is distributed among others including defense, railways, space department and psus
 chandrashekhar bataate hai, “sarkaar kii ranneeti yah he ki pratispardhaa paidaa kii jaae or nilaamiyon ke madhyam se spectrum se paisa banaaya jaae
 The government wants everyone to make proper use of spectrum
 yah aseem nahin he
 You have to innovate and provide for better services & this is the legitimate objective of public policy
 ”maamle ko badtar banane kaa kaam tenency anupaat kar rahaa he
 This is the number of operators who have installed their antennas per tower
 yah sankhya 2014-15 ke 1
 2 from 2020 to 77
 48 par pahunch jaaegi, jaisaa ki deloit kii ek report kaa kahana he
 The main reason for this is the increasing use of data
 mana ja rahaa he ki 2ji, 3ji or 4ji tenent kii sankhya 2020 tak 12,68,000 ho jaaegi, haalanki iske mukaable toweron ke badaae kii dar dhimi rahegi
 The report says that by 2020 the total number of towers will be 5,11,000
 deloit india ke senior diarector rajat banerjee kehete hai, “bharat data kranti ke muhane par khadaa he, lihaaja yahaan tower udyog ke bhavishya kii ore dekhne kaa yah sahi vakt he
 Due to the increasing use of smartphones among the people in the country, the data will grow at a qualitative pace which will require a substantial number of additional data sites
 ”deloit kaa adhyayan kahata he ki oparator ab 4ji network chaalu kar ke apni network kawarej kaa vistaar kar rahe hai or apni 3ji upasthiti ko bhi badha rahe hai
 Due to increased data usage driven coverage, the independent towers stand alone for data services are expected to have a compounded annual growth rate of 125 per cent by 2020, while other towers will be 1 for the next five years
 89 fisadi kii dar se badhenge
 Currently, the number of independent towers for just 3G and 4G is around 700
 wais upyog kii vruddhi main ai giravat se yah ashanka bhi saamne aa rahi he ki kahin swatantra toweron ke kaarobaar par asar na padane lag jaae
 However, the growth in data services itself will contribute to the growth of towers in the future and will pave the way for internal solutions and small cell sites
 bazaar main badhati pratispardhaa ke saath ab companiyon kaa jor apane graahakon ko badhaane par nahin balki sakriy upabhoktaaon ke aadhaar ko sudhaarney par he
 Regulation and Accountability One solution is to increase the towers
 iske liye companiyon ko apni jeb dhili kerani hogi
 Now with the introduction of 4G network, the existing capacity will be insufficient and the load on it will increase, so more towers will become an imperative
 kuch logon kaa kahana he ki bharat ko aise toweron ke saath prayog karnaa chahie jinase kam urja kii khapat hoti he, lekin janata ke bich jaagrukta kaarykram chalaakar unhen raji karne ke baad zyada ghaney tareeke se in toweron ko sthapit karnaa chahie
 This will solve both radiation fear and call drop problems
 tri ko bhi un companiyon ke maamle main sakchat hona hoga jo kuch cirkilon main baari kol drop kii dar ke saath batch nikalati hai kyonki rashtriya ausat isse bhi neeche hota he
 One way of doing this is to make the call quality within the circles accountable to service providers
 tri ko doorsanchaar udyog par najar rakhane ke liye banaaya gaya tha lekin iske aalochakon kaa kahana he ki is sanstha ne apni dhar kho di he
